#cheat All taxi guys are snowmen
//ID: 6085
//Score: 108
//Author: Waterbottle
//Category: Pedestrians
//Description: This makes all taxi drivers white. Change into ped 9 to be it
//Image: none
//Time: 03/04/2006 00:05:23
//Working: Yes

setchar(09b460de, 2) //hat
setchar(09b460ae, 2) //shirt
setchar(09b4613e, 2) //pants
setchar(09b4616e, 2) //shoes
setchar(09b4610e, 2) //hands
setchar(09b4601e, 2) //part of jacket
setchar(09b45fee, 2) //part of jacket
setchar(09b45fbe, 2) //part of jacket
setchar(09b45f8e, 2) //part of jacket
setchar(09b45f5e, 2) //part of jacket
setchar(09b45f2e, 2) //part of jacket
setchar(09b4604e, 2) //part of jacket
#off

setchar(09b460de, 3)
setchar(09b460ae, 2)
setchar(09b4613e, 5)
setchar(09b4616e, 6)
setchar(09b4610e, 4)
